<td> <h2>Welcome!</h2> <p><br>The Erzya language ( , <i>erz ke</i>), also Erzian or historically Arisa, is spoken by approximately 300,000 people in the northern, eastern and north-western parts of the Republic of Mordovia and adjacent regions of Chuvashia, Tatarstan, Bashkortostan, Penza, Samara, Nizhny Novgorod, Ulyanovsk etc.<br><br>The language belongs to the Mordvinic branch of the Uralic languages. Erzya is currently written using Cyrillic with no modifications to the variant used by the Russian language. In Mordovia, Erzya is co-official with Moksha and Russian.<br><br>Source: Wikipedia</p> </td> <td> <h2>Parois sovado!</h2> <p><br>Erz ke te uralo ke, kona sovavtovi suomi-ugra semijan suomi-ravo taradonte. Erz kels kort erzt. Rossijaso erztnede 2010 ije lovnomason tekst erz kelen koda tirineks 36 726 loma, snst ejst lamotne eri Mordovija Respublikaso. Erz kelente vesemede malaviks kele moko ke. Ikele s lovovs vejke mordva kele dialektks.<br><br>Erz kele ati eslempele keleks Mordovijaso, ruzo d moko keltne marto. Eslempele ormadoma koje ruzo kirilic, teke marto nauka literaturaso sejedst noldtnevi tevs lamo lija, latinic langs neede sistemat.<br><br>Limapr: Wikipedia</p> </td> </tr> </table> </div> </body> </html>Aleksanteri Nazarenkohttps://www.blogger.com/profile/13820160367271676349noreply@blogger.comtag:blogger.com,1999:blog-6110901624489546749.page-59052394331247238272024-02-23T17:58:00.002+02:002024-08-21T17:49:26.596+03:00About the spelling<br /><p>The Romanized version of the Erzya language used in this dictionary is loosely based on the proposal used in the book by linguists Ksenija Djordjevi and Jean-Lo Lonard, <a href="https://books.google.pl/books/about/Parlons_mordve.html?id=UTdXBLgYI_gC&amp;redir_esc=y">Parlons mordve (erzya et moka)</a>.<br /><br /> The transliteration tool may have some shortcomings due to the limitations of the Cyrillic script. It is recommended to use combinations like <i></i>, <i></i>, and <i></i> in compound words such as <i></i> (+), <i></i> (+), and <i></i> (+), and to avoid Russicisms where possible.<br><br> Moreover, the tool supports only Sentence case and lower case. UPPER CASE will not work correctly!</p>Aleksanteri Nazarenkohttps://www.blogger.com/profile/13820160367271676349noreply@blogger.comtag:blogger.com,1999:blog-6110901624489546749.page-29457639289590155352024-08-21T12:41:00.000+03:002024-08-21T12:41:28.819+03:00Finnish-Erzya dictionary <html lang="en"> <head> <meta charset="UTF-8"></meta> <meta content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" name="viewport"></meta> <link href="styles.css" rel="stylesheet"></link> <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Cantarell:wght@400;700&amp;display=swap" rel="stylesheet"></link> <title>Dictionary</title> </head> <body> <div class="container"> <select id="languageSelector"> <option value="latin">Latin</option> <option value="cyrillic">Cyrillic</option> </select> <input id="searchInput" placeholder="Search for a word ..." type="text" /> <ul id="dictionaryList"></ul> </div> <script src="script.js"></script> </body> </html> <style> body { font-family: 'Verdana', sans-serif; font-size: 16px; margin: 0; padding: 0; } .container { max-width: 800px; margin: 0 auto; padding: 20px; background-color: transparent; box-shadow: none; } h1 { text-align: center; } #searchInput { font-family: 'Verdana', sans-serif; font-size: 16px; width: 100%; padding: 10px; margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px; border: 1px solid #ccc; border-radius: 5px; } ul { list-style-type: none; padding: 0; margin: 0; } li { padding: 15px 10px; line-height: 2; border-bottom: none; background-color: transparent; } .word { font-weight: regular; font-size: 16px; } .definition { font-style: italic; font-size: 16px; } #languageSelector { font-family: 'Verdana', sans-serif; margin-bottom: 20px; padding: 5px; font-size: 16px; } </style> <script> document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => { const latinJsonURL = 'https://raw.githubusercontent.com/aleksanterinazarenko/dictionary.json/main/dictionary3.json'; const cyrillicJsonURL = 'https://raw.githubusercontent.com/aleksanterinazarenko/dictionary.json/main/dictionary3-cyr.json'; const dictionaryList = document.getElementById('dictionaryList'); const searchInput = document.getElementById('searchInput'); const languageSelector = document.getElementById('languageSelector'); let currentData = []; // Function to render the dictionary list function renderList(words) { dictionaryList.innerHTML = ''; words.forEach(entry => { const listItem = document.createElement('li'); listItem.className = 'entry'; listItem.innerHTML = `<span class="word">${entry.Word}</span>: <span class="definition">${entry.Definition}</span>`; dictionaryList.appendChild(listItem); }); } // Function to calculate similarity based on common prefix length function getSimilarityScore(word, query) { let score = 0; for (let i = 0; i < Math.min(word.length, query.length); i++) { if (word[i] === query[i]) { score++; } else { break; } } return score; } // Function to load the dictionary data function loadDictionary(url) { fetch(url) .then(response => { if (!response.ok) { throw new Error('Network response was not ok'); } return response.json(); }) .then(data => { currentData = data; dictionaryList.innerHTML = ''; // Clear the list when data is loaded }) .catch(error => console.error('Error loading the dictionary:', error)); } // Search functionality searchInput.addEventListener('input', (event) => { const query = event.target.value.toLowerCase(); if (query === "") { dictionaryList.innerHTML = ''; // Clear the list if the search query is empty } else { const filteredWords = currentData .filter(entry => entry.Word.toLowerCase().includes(query)) .sort((a, b) => { const scoreA = getSimilarityScore(a.Word.toLowerCase(), query); const scoreB = getSimilarityScore(b.Word.toLowerCase(), query); return scoreB - scoreA; // Sort by similarity score (descending) }); renderList(filteredWords); // Render the filtered words } }); // Handle language change languageSelector.addEventListener('change', (event) => { const selectedLanguage = event.target.value;
